This Dehradun bungalow costing 16 crores and spread over 10 acres has been considered as 'ill-fated' or 'cursed'
 trivendra singh ravat se pehle mukhyamantri kii kursi sanbhaalane vaale harish ravat is bangale main rahane kii jagah rajya sarkaar ke ek guest house main hi rah kar apana kaam chalaate rahe the

 bataa den ki mukhyamantri rahete ramesh pokharial nishank (may 2011 se sitambar 2011), bisi khanduri (sintabar 2011 se march 2012) or vijay bahuguna (march 2012 se janvari 2014) is ghar main rah chuke hai lekin teenon hi apana kaarykaal puraa nahin kar paae
 Trivendra Singh Rawat entered the bungalow after reciting the general pooja related to home entry
 unka parivaar 60 main se sirf 5 kamaron kaa istemaal karegaa
 No expensive furniture will be used in the bungalow
 iske alaava pani kii barbaadi ko rokane ke liye siem ne bangale ke swimming pool ko bhi band karne kaa aadesh diya he

 The husband of a minor girl is entitled to the right of protection of his wife, but he cannot have a physical relationship with his wife until he is 20 years old
 aisa karne par kanoon uski patni ko apni shaadi ko amaanya ghoshit karne ke liye adaalat kaa darwaja khatkhatane kii anumati detaa he
 a three-member bench of the Delhi High Court gave this arrangement in response to a reference of a two-member bench
 usamen poocha gaya tha ki kya yah kaha ja saktaa he ki koi naaballig ladki samajhadaari kii umr main aa gai he or vah apane mata-pita kii vidhisammat sangrakshan se baahar nikal sakati he
 a bench of Acting Chief Justice AK Sikri, Justice Sanjeev Khanna and Justice VK Shali said, "we are of the opinion that since the marriage is not invalid, the husband is automatically entitled to the right to look after the minor girl
" peeth ne kaha, lekin, pati ko vivaah ko purna banane ke liye shaareerik sambandh banane kii anumati dena uchit nahin ho saktaa, jab pisiem (bal vivaah nirodhak) adhinium kaa uddeshy or tarkaadhar he ki kam umr main kisi bachche kii shaadi nahin honi chahie, kyonki ve manovaigyanik yaa chikitsiya taur par shaadi ke yogya nahin hote
 "ultimately, such a marriage is voidable and the girl still has the option of knocking on the court to declare the marriage invalid until she is 20 years old," the bench said
 adaalat ne yah bhi kaha, kaise vah is bich apane adhikaar kaa istemaal karne main sakasham hogi, jab shaadi ko purna banane ke liye usase shaareerik sambandh bana liya jaataa he, jabaki vah sahmati dene kii sthiti main nahin he, jisase vah garbhvatee ho sakati he or garbhadhaaran kar sakati he
 If such marriages are made legally enforceable, it can have a fatal effect and it will not stop anyone from getting married like this
 tippaniyan The bench also responded to another question of the two-member bench on whether the marriage of a boy under 21 years of age to a girl under 18 years of age can be said to be valid and if the husband is not in jail, should he Protection of the girl can be given
 adaalat ne kaha ki naaballig ladki or ladke ke bich shaadi ko avaidh ghoshit kiya ja saktaa he, basharte pati-patni main se koi balig hone se pehle adaalat kaa darwaja khatkhataaye
 The bench said, marriage between a girl below 18 years of age or a boy under 21 years of age would not be invalid, but it would be voidable if such a child does not take any step to declare her marriage invalid
 Is, then that marriage will become legal
 dilli hoicourt kii teen-sadasyeey peeth ne yah vyavastha do-sadasyeey peeth ke ek reference ke jawaab main di
 It asked whether it could be said that a minor girl had reached the age of prudence and that she could get out of the legal protection of her parents
 kaaryvahak mukhya nyaayadhish eke sikri, nyaayamurti sanjeev khanna or nyaayamurti wike shaali kii peeth ne kaha, hamaari yah raay he ki chunki shaadi amaanya nahin he, isliye swat: pati naaballig ladki kii dekharekh kaa adhikaar paane kaa hakdaar he
 The bench said, however, it may not be appropriate to allow the husband to have a physical relationship to complete the marriage, when the purpose and rationale of the PCM (prevention of Child Marriage) Act is that no child should be married at a young age
 Because they are not psychologically or medically eligible for marriage
 peeth ne kaha, aakhirkaar is tarah kii shaadi nirast karne yogya he or ladki ke paas 20 saal kii umr hone tak ab bhi shaadi ko amaanya ghoshit karne ke liye adaalat kaa darwaja khatkhatane kaa vikalp he
 The court also said, how she would be able to exercise her authority in the meantime when a physical relationship is made with her to complete the marriage, while she is not in a position to give consent, which could lead to her becoming pregnant
 And can conceive
 is tarah kii shaadiyon ko agar kanuunan lagu karne yogya banaaya gaya, to iskaa ghaatak prabhaav ho saktaa he or yah is tarah kii shaadi karne se kisi ko bhi nahin rokegaa
 The comments peeth ne do-sadasyeey peeth ke ek anya sawaal kaa bhi jawaab diya ki kya 21 saal se kam umr ke ladke kii 18 saal se kam umr kii ladki se shaadi ko vaid kaha ja saktaa he or agar pati jail main nahin he, to kya use ladki kaa sangrakshan diya ja saktaa he
 The court said that marriage between a minor girl and a boy can be declared invalid, provided one of the spouses knocks before the court
 peeth ne kaha, 18 saal se kam umr kii ladki yaa 21 saal se kam umr ke ladke bich hui shaadi amaanya nahin hogi, balki yah amaanya karne yogya hogi, agar is tarah kaa baccha apni shaadi ko amaanya ghoshit karwaane ke liye koi kadam nahin uthaata he, to vah shaadi vaid ho jaaegi

 About Chandrayaan-2 How many days orbiter - 1 year, Lander (vikram) - 15 days, Rover (pragyan) - 15 days Total weight of the mission: 3877 kg Orbiter - 2379 kg, Lander (vikram) - 1471 kg, Rover (pragyan) - 27 kg orbiter: isro's mobile command center 100 km above the moon, the orbiter of Chandrayaan-2 will send the information received from the lander and rover to ISRO center, orbiting 100 km above the moon
 saath hi isro se bheje gaye cmand ko lander or rover tak pahunchayegaa

 Why it took 11 years for the launch of Chandrayaan-2 In November 2007, the Russian space agency Rosskosmos said that it would work together in this project
 vah isro ko lander degaa

 The launch was scheduled in January 2013, but the Russian space agency rosscosmos lander could not deliver
 phir isaki lonching 2016 main tay kii gai
 However, in 2015, Rosskosmos withdrew from the project

 in mahilaon ne sarkaar se apil kii, un logon ko insaaf milanaa chahie

 ye yachika hindu ladki kii muslim ladke se shaadi ke masale ko lekar daayar kii gai he

 Judith Prochaska, an assistant professor at Stanford University in the United States and the leader of this research, said in a statement, "health losses from smoking have been known for centuries, but the findings of this research have revealed the financial harm from smoking
" 
 " In this new research, Judith and her team studied 131 unemployed non-smoking participants and 120 unemployed non-smoking participants for a year
